>     <script>> 
>         // ── 모바일 메뉴 토글 ───────────────────────────────────────────> 
>         const mobileMenuButton = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-button');> 
>         const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('mobile-menu');> 
>         if (mobileMenuButton) {> 
>             mobileMenuButton.addEventListener('click', () => mobileMenu.classList.toggle('hidden'));> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         // ── 네비게이션 활성화 ──────────────────────────────────────────> 
>         const currentPath = window.location.pathname.split('/').pop();> 
>         document.querySelectorAll('.nav-link, .mobile-nav-link').forEach(link => {> 
>             const lp = link.getAttribute('href');> 
>             if (lp === currentPath || (currentPath === '' && lp === 'main.html')) {> 
>                 link.classList.add('text-primary', 'font-bold');> 
>                 link.classList.remove('text-on-surface-variant');> 
>             }> 
>         });> 
> > 
>         // ── 미구현 기능 팝업 ───────────────────────────────────────────> 
>         function handleUnavailableFeature() {> 
>             alert('현재 이 기능은 고도화 단계에 있습니다. 업데이트 이후 사용 가능하니 잠시만 기다려주세요.');> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         // ── 사이드바 메뉴 항목 연결 ────────────────────────────────────> 
>         document.querySelectorAll('nav .menu-item').forEach(item => {> 
>             const text = item.textContent.trim();> 
>             if (text.includes('로그아웃')) {> 
>                 item.addEventListener('click', async e => {> 
>                     e.preventDefault();> 
>                     try { await fetch('/api/auth/logout', { method: 'POST', credentials: 'same-origin' }); } catch (_) {}> 
>                     window.location.href = '/';> 
>                 });> 
>             } else if (item.id === 'security-menu-item') {> 
>                 item.addEventListener('click', e => { e.preventDefault(); openSecurityModal(); });> 
>             } else {> 
>                 item.addEventListener('click', e => { e.preventDefault(); handleUnavailableFeature(); });> 
>             }> 
>         });> 
> > 
>         // ── 계정 삭제 버튼 ─────────────────────────────────────────────> 
>         document.querySelectorAll('button').forEach(btn => {> 
>             if (btn.textContent.trim().includes('계정 삭제')) btn.addEventListener('click', handleUnavailableFeature);> 
>         });> 
> > 
>         // ── 아바타 표시 헬퍼 ───────────────────────────────────────────> 
>         function applyAvatar(avatarUrl) {> 
>             // 프로필 카드 대형 아바타> 
>             const icon = document.getElementById('profile-avatar-icon');> 
>             const img  = document.getElementById('profile-avatar-img');> 
>             if (avatarUrl && img) {> 
>                 img.src = avatarUrl + '?t=' + Date.now();> 
>                 img.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                 if (icon) icon.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             } else if (icon) {> 
>                 icon.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                 if (img) img.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             }> 
>             // 네비게이션 소형 아바타> 
>             const navIcon = document.getElementById('nav-avatar-icon');> 
>             const navImg  = document.getElementById('nav-avatar-img');> 
>             if (avatarUrl && navImg) {> 
>                 navImg.src = avatarUrl + '?t=' + Date.now();> 
>                 navImg.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                 if (navIcon) navIcon.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             } else if (navIcon) {> 
>                 navIcon.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                 if (navImg) navImg.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             }> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         // ── 사용자 정보 로드 ───────────────────────────────────────────> 
>         let _currentUser = null;> 
> > 
>         (async function loadUserData() {> 
>             try {> 
>                 const [meRes, statsRes, resumesRes] = await Promise.all([> 
>                     fetch('/api/auth/me', { credentials: 'same-origin' }),> 
>                     fetch('/api/stats',   { credentials: 'same-origin' }),> 
>                     fetch('/api/resumes', { credentials: 'same-origin' })> 
>                 ]);> 
> > 
>                 const meData = await meRes.json();> 
>                 if (meData.success && meData.user) {> 
>                     _currentUser = meData.user;> 
>                     const u = meData.user;> 
>                     const nameEl   = document.getElementById('profile-name');> 
>                     const emailEl  = document.getElementById('profile-email');> 
>                     const joinedEl = document.getElementById('profile-joined');> 
>                     const roleEl   = document.getElementById('profile-role');> 
>                     if (nameEl)   nameEl.textContent  = u.name  || '이름 없음';> 
>                     if (emailEl)  emailEl.textContent = u.email || '—';> 
>                     if (joinedEl) {> 
>                         const d = u.created_at ? new Date(u.created_at) : null;> 
>                         joinedEl.textContent = d ? `${d.getFullYear()}년 ${d.getMonth()+1}월 ${d.getDate()}일` : '—';> 
>                     }> 
>                     if (roleEl && u.is_admin) roleEl.textContent = 'a4u 관리자';> 
>                     applyAvatar(u.avatar_url);> 
>                 } else if (meRes.status === 401) {> 
>                     window.location.href = 'login.html?next=profile-menu.html&reason=auth';> 
>                     return;> 
>                 }> 
> > 
>                 const statsData = await statsRes.json();> 
>                 if (statsData.success) {> 
>                     const s = statsData.stats;> 
>                     const rEl = document.getElementById('stat-resumes');> 
>                     const aEl = document.getElementById('stat-applications');> 
>                     const uEl = document.getElementById('stat-uploads');> 
>                     if (rEl) rEl.textContent = s.total_resumes      ?? 0;> 
>                     if (aEl) aEl.textContent = s.total_applications ?? 0;> 
>                     if (uEl) uEl.textContent = s.total_uploads       ?? 0;> 
>                 }> 
> > 
>                 const resumesData = await resumesRes.json();> 
>                 const activityContainer = document.querySelector('.space-y-3');> 
>                 if (activityContainer && resumesData.success && resumesData.resumes?.length > 0) {> 
>                     const recent = resumesData.resumes.filter(r => !r.is_sample).slice(0, 3);> 
>                     if (recent.length > 0) {> 
>                         activityContainer.innerHTML = recent.map(r => {> 
>                             const dt = r.updated_at || r.created_at;> 
>                             const d  = dt ? new Date(dt) : new Date();> 
>                             const dateStr = `${d.getFullYear()}년 ${d.getMonth()+1}월 ${d.getDate()}일`;> 
>                             return `<div class="flex items-start gap-3 pb-3 border-b last:border-b-0">> 
>                                 <span class="material-symbols-outlined text-blue-600 flex-shrink-0">article</span>> 
>                                 <div><p class="font-medium text-gray-900">${r.title || '이력서'} 수정됨</p>> 
>                                 <p class="text-sm text-gray-500">${dateStr}</p></div></div>`;> 
>                         }).join('');> 
>                     } else {> 
>                         activityContainer.innerHTML = `<p class="text-sm text-gray-500 text-center py-4">아직 활동 내역이 없습니다.</p>`;> 
>                     }> 
>                 } else if (activityContainer) {> 
>                     activityContainer.innerHTML = `<p class="text-sm text-gray-500 text-center py-4">아직 활동 내역이 없습니다.</p>`;> 
>                 }> 
>             } catch (err) {> 
>                 console.warn('프로필 데이터 로드 실패:', err);> 
>             }> 
>         })();> 
> > 
>         // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════> 
>         // 프로필 수정 모달> 
>         // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════> 
>         // ── 아바타 미리보기 (파일 선택 시 즉시 업로드) ────────────────> 
>         async function previewAvatar(input) {> 
>             if (!input.files || !input.files[0]) return;> 
>             const file = input.files[0];> 
> > 
>             // 미리보기 표시> 
>             const reader = new FileReader();> 
>             reader.onload = e => {> 
>                 const prevIcon = document.getElementById('pm-avatar-preview-icon');> 
>                 const prevImg  = document.getElementById('pm-avatar-preview-img');> 
>                 if (prevImg) { prevImg.src = e.target.result; prevImg.classList.remove('hidden'); }> 
>                 if (prevIcon) prevIcon.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             };> 
>             reader.readAsDataURL(file);> 
> > 
>             // 즉시 서버 업로드> 
>             document.getElementById('pm-avatar-uploading').classList.remove('hidden');> 
>             const fd = new FormData();> 
>             fd.append('avatar', file);> 
>             try {> 
>                 const r    = await fetch('/api/auth/avatar', { method: 'POST', credentials: 'same-origin', body: fd });> 
>                 const data = await r.json();> 
>                 if (data.success) {> 
>                     _currentUser = data.user;> 
>                     applyAvatar(data.avatar_url);> 
>                 } else {> 
>                     alert(data.message || '이미지 업로드에 실패했습니다.');> 
>                 }> 
>             } catch (_) {> 
>                 alert('네트워크 오류가 발생했습니다.');> 
>             } finally {> 
>                 document.getElementById('pm-avatar-uploading').classList.add('hidden');> 
>             }> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         function openProfileModal() {> 
>             document.getElementById('pm-error').classList.add('hidden');> 
>             document.getElementById('pm-success').classList.add('hidden');> 
>             document.getElementById('pm-current-pw').value = '';> 
>             document.getElementById('pm-avatar-input').value = '';> 
> > 
>             // 모달 내 아바타 미리보기 초기화> 
>             const prevIcon = document.getElementById('pm-avatar-preview-icon');> 
>             const prevImg  = document.getElementById('pm-avatar-preview-img');> 
>             if (_currentUser && _currentUser.avatar_url) {> 
>                 if (prevImg) { prevImg.src = _currentUser.avatar_url; prevImg.classList.remove('hidden'); }> 
>                 if (prevIcon) prevIcon.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             } else {> 
>                 if (prevImg) prevImg.classList.add('hidden');> 
>                 if (prevIcon) prevIcon.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>             }> 
> > 
>             if (_currentUser) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('pm-name').value  = _currentUser.name  || '';> 
>                 document.getElementById('pm-email').value = _currentUser.email || '';> 
>             }> 
>             document.getElementById('profile-modal').classList.remove('hidden');> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         function closeProfileModal() {> 
>             document.getElementById('profile-modal').classList.add('hidden');> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         async function saveProfile() {> 
>             const btn      = document.getElementById('pm-save-btn');> 
>             const errEl    = document.getElementById('pm-error');> 
>             const succEl   = document.getElementById('pm-success');> 
>             errEl.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             succEl.classList.add('hidden');> 
> > 
>             const name       = document.getElementById('pm-name').value.trim();> 
>             const email      = document.getElementById('pm-email').value.trim();> 
>             const currentPw  = document.getElementById('pm-current-pw').value;> 
> > 
>             if (!name || !email) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('pm-error-msg').textContent = '이름과 이메일을 모두 입력해주세요.';> 
>                 errEl.classList.remove('hidden'); return;> 
>             }> 
>             if (!currentPw) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('pm-error-msg').textContent = '현재 비밀번호를 입력해주세요.';> 
>                 errEl.classList.remove('hidden'); return;> 
>             }> 
> > 
>             btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = '저장 중...';> 
>             try {> 
>                 const r = await fetch('/api/auth/profile', {> 
>                     method: 'PUT',> 
>                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },> 
>                     credentials: 'same-origin',> 
>                     body: JSON.stringify({ name, email, current_password: currentPw })> 
>                 });> 
>                 const data = await r.json();> 
>                 if (data.success) {> 
>                     _currentUser = data.user;> 
>                     document.getElementById('profile-name').textContent  = data.user.name;> 
>                     document.getElementById('profile-email').textContent = data.user.email;> 
>                     succEl.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                     setTimeout(() => closeProfileModal(), 1500);> 
>                 } else {> 
>                     document.getElementById('pm-error-msg').textContent = data.message || '저장에 실패했습니다.';> 
>                     errEl.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                 }> 
>             } catch (_) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('pm-error-msg').textContent = '네트워크 오류가 발생했습니다.';> 
>                 errEl.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>             } finally {> 
>                 btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '저장';> 
>             }> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════> 
>         // 보안 설정 모달 (비밀번호 변경)> 
>         // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════> 
>         function openSecurityModal() {> 
>             ['sc-current-pw','sc-new-pw','sc-confirm-pw'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');> 
>             document.getElementById('sc-error').classList.add('hidden');> 
>             document.getElementById('sc-success').classList.add('hidden');> 
>             document.getElementById('security-modal').classList.remove('hidden');> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         function closeSecurityModal() {> 
>             document.getElementById('security-modal').classList.add('hidden');> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         async function changePassword() {> 
>             const btn     = document.getElementById('sc-save-btn');> 
>             const errEl   = document.getElementById('sc-error');> 
>             const succEl  = document.getElementById('sc-success');> 
>             errEl.classList.add('hidden');> 
>             succEl.classList.add('hidden');> 
> > 
>             const currentPw = document.getElementById('sc-current-pw').value;> 
>             const newPw     = document.getElementById('sc-new-pw').value;> 
>             const confirmPw = document.getElementById('sc-confirm-pw').value;> 
> > 
>             if (!currentPw || !newPw || !confirmPw) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('sc-error-msg').textContent = '모든 항목을 입력해주세요.';> 
>                 errEl.classList.remove('hidden'); return;> 
>             }> 
>             if (newPw !== confirmPw) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('sc-error-msg').textContent = '새 비밀번호가 일치하지 않습니다.';> 
>                 errEl.classList.remove('hidden'); return;> 
>             }> 
> > 
>             btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = '변경 중...';> 
>             try {> 
>                 const r = await fetch('/api/auth/change-password', {> 
>                     method: 'PUT',> 
>                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },> 
>                     credentials: 'same-origin',> 
>                     body: JSON.stringify({ current_password: currentPw, new_password: newPw, confirm_password: confirmPw })> 
>                 });> 
>                 const data = await r.json();> 
>                 if (data.success) {> 
>                     succEl.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                     setTimeout(() => closeSecurityModal(), 1800);> 
>                 } else {> 
>                     document.getElementById('sc-error-msg').textContent = data.message || '변경에 실패했습니다.';> 
>                     errEl.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>                 }> 
>             } catch (_) {> 
>                 document.getElementById('sc-error-msg').textContent = '네트워크 오류가 발생했습니다.';> 
>                 errEl.classList.remove('hidden');> 
>             } finally {> 
>                 btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '변경';> 
>             }> 
>         }> 
> > 
>         // ESC 키로 모달 닫기> 
>         document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {> 
>             if (e.key === 'Escape') { closeProfileModal(); closeSecurityModal(); }> 
>         });> 
>     </script>> 
> </body>> 
> </html>> 
>

>                     <a href="main.html" class="nav-link font-body-md text-on-surface-variant hover:text-primary transition-colors">메인</a>>

>                     <a href="select.html" class="nav-link font-body-md text-on-surface-variant hover:text-primary transition-colors">제출 관리</a>>

>             <div class="flex items-center gap-4">> 
>                 <button class="p-2 text-on-surface-variant hover:text-primary transition-colors hidden sm:block">> 
>                     <span class="material-symbols-outlined">notifications</span>>
